	На $\widetilde D = \Cm \setminus \{z \in \Cm: \Im z = 0,\ \Re z \geqslant 0 \}$ можно выделить $n$ однозначных ветвей.
	\[ f_k(z) = \sqrt[n]{|z|} e^\frac{i(\arg z + 2 \pi k)}{n},\ k = 0, 1, \ldots, n-1 \]
	$w = f_0(z)$ --- конформно на $\widetilde{D}$
	\newpage
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (0:1.5) arc (0:135:1.5) -- cycle;
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) -- (135:1.5);
				\draw[thick] (0.3,0) arc (0:135:0.3);
				\node at (0.4,0.5) {$\dfrac{2\pi}{n}$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\subsection{Отображения, задаваемые функциями $f(z) = e^z$, $f(z) = \operatorname{Ln}(z)$}
	\subsubsection{Функция $ f(z) = e^z $}
	Её производная $f'(z) = e^z \neq 0, \ \forall z \in \Cm \Rightarrow f(z) \in \A(\Cm)$, она конформна на $\Cm$.\\
	$e^z = e^{x + iy} \Rightarrow |e^z| = e^x$\\
	$\forall z \in \Cm \Rightarrow e^z = e^{z + 2\pi i},\ T = 2\pi i$ --- основной период\\
	Уравнение $e^z = 0$ не имеет решений.
	\[ D = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 < \Im z < 2\pi\} \text{ --- область конформности.} \]
	(Любая полоса шириной $ 2\pi $ является облостью конформности.)
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			% Левый рисунок
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (1.5,1);
				
				\fill (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};
				\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
				\node at (0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_2$};
				\node at (-0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_3$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Парметризуем границы этой области:
	$ \begin{cases}
		\Gamma_1: z = x,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = e^x\\
		\Gamma_2: z = x + 2 \pi i,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = e^x\\
		\Gamma_3: z = x + \pi i,\ x \in \R \Rightarrow w = -e^x
	\end{cases} $
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm :\ 0 < \arg w < 2\pi \} \]
	\newpage
	\subsection*{Примеры}
	\noindent\textbf{1)} 
	$ D_z = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 \leqslant \Im z \leqslant 2\pi,\ \Re z \leqslant 0 \} $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				% Левый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (0,1);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (0,1);
					\node at (-0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
					\node at (-0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_3$};
					\node at (0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_2$};
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				% Правый рисунок
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(0,0) circle (0.75)
						(0,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
					\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) circle (0.75);
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				% Стрелка между рисунками
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	$ \begin{cases}
		\Gamma_1: z = x,\ x \leqslant 0 \Rightarrow w = e^x \\
		\Gamma_2: z = yi,\  0 \leqslant y \leqslant 2\pi \Rightarrow w = e^{iy}\\
		\Gamma_3: z = x + 2\pi i,\ x \leqslant 0 \Rightarrow w = e^x
	\end{cases} $
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: |w| < 1\} \setminus \{ w \in \Cm: \Im w = 0,\ 0 \leqslant \Re w \leqslant 1 \} \]
	\noindent\textbf{2)} $ D_z = \{z \in \Cm :\ 0 \leqslant \Im z \leqslant 2\pi,\ \Re z \geqslant 0 \} $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				% Левый рисунок

					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0, 1) -- (1.5,1);
					\node at (0.6,-0.15) {$\Gamma_1$};
					\node at (0.6,1.15) {$\Gamma_3$};
					\node at (-0.15,0.5) {$\Gamma_2$};
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$2\pi i$};

				\end{scope}
				% Правый рисунок

				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Знаем, что вся полоса перейдет на плоскость с разрезом. Выше увидили, что левая половина перешла на круг с разрезом, а значит правая полоса перейдет во внешность окружности с разрезом.
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: |w| > 1\} \setminus \{ w \in \Cm: \Im w = 0,\ \Re w \geqslant 1 \} \]\newpage
	\noindent\textbf{3)} Аналогичные примеры с более тонкой полоской.

	\begin{center}

					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (-1.5, 1) -- (0,1);
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$\pi i$};

					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill[black] (-0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above left] {$-1$};
					\fill[black] (0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$1$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				% Стрелка между рисунками
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.5,1);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0, 1) -- (1.5,1);
					\fill[black] (0,1) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$\pi i$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}

					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-0.75,0) arc (180:0:0.75) -- cycle
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\end{scope}

				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\newpage
	\subsubsection{Функция $ f(z) = \operatorname{Ln}z $}
	\noindent
	\[ \operatorname{Ln}z = \ln{|z|} + i(\arg z +2\pi k)\text{ --- бесконечно-значная функция} \]
	\noindent
	$w = f_0(z)=\ln z=\ln{|z|} + i \arg z $ --- Главная ветвь.(Оно конформно в $ D_z $)\\
	$D_z = \Cm \setminus \{z \in \Cm: \Im z = 0,\ \Re z \geqslant 0 \}$
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]

					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5) % вся плоскость
					(0, -0.05) rectangle (1.5, 0.05); % луч (вычитается)
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};

			\end{scope}

			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)

		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\[ D_w= \{ w \in \Cm : 0 < \Im w < 2\pi i \} \]
	\subsection{Отображение задаваемые функцией Жуковского}
	\[ f(z) = \frac{1}{2} (z + \frac{1}{z}) \]
	Найдем ее производную: $f'(z) = \dfrac{1}{2} (1 - \dfrac{1}{z^2})$. Производная не равна 0, при $z \neq \pm 1.$ \\ \noindent
	Очевидно, что $0 \mapsto \infty$ и $\infty \mapsto \infty$.
	 
	Рассмотрим $z_1 = 0$ и отображение $\dfrac{1}{f(z)}$
	\[ \frac{1}{f(z)} = \frac{2}{z + \frac{1}{z}} = \frac{2z}{z^2 + 1} = g(z) \Rightarrow g'(0) = 2 \Rightarrow w = f(z) \text{ конформно в точке } 0.\]
	
	Рассмотрим $z_2 = \infty$. Обозначим $s = \dfrac{1}{z}$. Тогда
	\[ h(s) = \frac{1}{2}(\frac{1}{s} + s) \Rightarrow h(s)\text{ конформно в точке } 0 \Rightarrow w = f(z) \text{ конформно в точке } \infty/ \]
	\textbf{Вывод:} отображение $ f(z) = \dfrac{1}{2} (z + \dfrac{1}{z}) $ конформно в каждой точке, кроме $ z = \pm 1 $
	\newpage
	\section{Лекция 12}
	\begin{statement}
		Функция Жуковского может быть записана как композиция двух следующих функций: 
		$w_1 = \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}$ и $w_2 = w_1^2$.
	\end{statement}
	\begin{proof}
		\[ w = \frac{1 + w_2}{1 - w_2} = \frac{1 + \left( \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}\right) ^2}{1 - \left( \dfrac{z - 1}{z + 1}\right) ^2} = \frac{2z^2 + 2}{4z} = \frac{1}{2}\left( z + \frac{1}{z}\right)  \]
	\end{proof}
	\begin{statement}
		Отображение $ f(z) = \frac{1}{2} (z + \frac{1}{z})$, конформно в области $ D_z $, если
		$ D_z $ одновременно не содержит точек $ z_1,\ z_2 : z_1z_2 = 1$ и $ \pm 1 \notin D_z.$
	\end{statement}
	\begin{proof}
		Исследуем на взаимооднозначность при $ z_1 \ne z_2. $
		\[w_1 - w_2 = \frac{1}{2}\left( z_1 + \frac{1}{z_1}\right)  - \frac{1}{2}\left( z_2 + \frac{1}{z_2}\right) = \frac{z_1-z_2}{2}\left( 1-\frac{1}{z_1z_2} \right) \Rightarrow w_1 \ne w_1 \iff z_1z_2 \ne 1 \]
	\end{proof}
	\subsection{Примеры}
	\noindent \textbf{1)} $ D_z = \{ z\in \Cm: |z| < R, R < 1 \} $\\
	Параметрически предстваляем границу: $ z = Re^{i\phi},\ -\pi < \phi \leqslant \pi$
	\[  w = \frac{1}{2}(Re^{i\phi} + \frac{1}{R}e^{-i\phi}) = \frac{1}{2}(R(\cos\phi + i\sin\phi) + \frac{1}{R}(\cos\phi - i\sin\phi)) \] 
	$ \begin{cases}
		u(R,\, \phi) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left(R+\dfrac{1}{R}\right)\cos\phi\\
		v(R,\,\phi) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left(R-\dfrac{1}{R}\right)\sin\phi
	\end{cases} $, геометрическое место этих точек --- эллипс.
	\[ \dfrac{u^2}{\dfrac{1}{2^2}\left(R +\dfrac{1}{R} \right)^2 } + \dfrac{v^2}{\dfrac{1}{2^2}\left(R-\dfrac{1}{R} \right)^2 } = 1 \]
	\[ D_w = \{ w \in \Cm: \frac{4(\Re w)^2}{\left( R+\dfrac{1}{R}\right)^2} + \frac{4(\Im w)^2}{\left( R-\dfrac{1}{R}\right)^2} > 1 \} \]
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\draw[fill=blue!20]
					(0,0) circle (0.75);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node at (1.1,-0.15) {$R<1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(0,0) ellipse (1.2 and 0.75);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) ellipse (1.2 and 0.75);
				\fill[black] (0,0.75) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$\frac{1}{2}(R-\frac{1}{R}) $};
				\fill[black] (1.2,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$\frac{1}{2}(R+\frac{1}{R}) $};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\textbf{2)} $ D_z = \{ z\in \Cm: |z| \leqslant 1 \} $

	\textbf{5)} $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: \Im z > 0\} $\\
	Выполним анализ графика функции $ f(x) = \dfrac{1}{2}\left(x+\dfrac{1}{x}\right)  $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1]
			\begin{scope}
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-3,-3) rectangle (3,3);
					\draw[domain=-3:-0.1, smooth, variable=\x, blue, thick] 
					plot ({\x}, {0.5*(\x + 1/\x)});
					\draw[domain=0.1:3, smooth, variable=\x, blue, thick] 
					plot ({\x}, {0.5*(\x + 1/\x)});
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-3,0) -- (3,0) node[below] {$ x $};
				\draw[->] (0,-3) -- (0,3) node[below left] {$ y $};
				\draw[dashed] (1,0) -- (1,1);
				\draw[dashed] (0,1) -- (1,1);
				\draw[dashed] (-1,0) -- (-1,-1);
				\draw[dashed] (0,-1) -- (-1,-1);
				\fill (1,1) circle (1pt);
				\fill (-1,-1) circle (1pt);
				\node[below right] at (1,0) {$1$};
				\node[below left] at (0,1) {$1$};
				\node[below left] at (-1,0) {$-1$};
				\node[below right] at (0,-1) {$-1$};
			\end{scope}
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\begin{flalign*}
		&f' = \frac{1}{2}\left(1 - \frac{1}{x^2} \right) = 0 \Rightarrow x = \pm 1 \text{ экстремумы. }&\\
		&f'' = \frac{1}{x^2} \Rightarrow f''(1) = 1 > 0 \text{ --- выпукла вниз},\ f''(-1) = -1 > 0 \text{ --- выпукла вверх.}&
	\end{flalign*}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05)
					(0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05);
				\draw (0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\node[below left] at (0.75,0) {$1$};
				\node[below right] at (-0.75,0) {$-1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\[ D_w = \Cm \setminus \{ w \in \Cm : \Im w = 0,\ \Re w \leqslant 0 \} \cup \{ w \in \Cm : \Im w = 0,\ \Re w \geqslant 0 \} \]
	\textbf{6)} $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: \Im z < 0\} $\\
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,0);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05)
					(0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (-0.75,0.05);
				\draw (0.75,0.05) rectangle (1.5,-0.05);
				\node[below left] at (0.75,0) {$1$};
				\node[below right] at (-0.75,0) {$-1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\[ D_w = \Cm \setminus \{ w \in \Cm : \Im w = 0,\ \Re w \leqslant 0 \} \cup \{ w \in \Cm : \Im w = 0,\ \Re w \geqslant 0 \} \]
	\subsection{Отображение луночек и областей с разрывами}
	\begin{definition}
		\textbf{Луночка} --- область, граница которой имеет вид: $ \gamma_1 \cup \gamma_2 $, где  $ \gamma_1, \gamma_2 $ --- дуги обобщенных окружностей и
		$ \gamma_1 \cap \gamma_2 $ содержит две точки.
	\end{definition}
	\begin{example}
		Найти отображение, которое переводит $ D_z $ в $ D_w $, где\\ $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: |z| < 1,\ \Im z > 0 \}, \ D_w = \{ w\in\Cm: \Im w > 0 \}$
	\end{example}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\draw[fill=blue!20] (-0.75,0) arc (180:0:0.75) -- cycle;
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill[black] (-0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above left] {$-1$};
				\fill[black] (0.75,0) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			% Стрелка между рисунками
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Найдем отображение, которое переводит полуокружность в угол с центром в начале координат, для этого $ -1\mapsto 0 $ и $ 1\mapsto \infty $.\\
	Получим $ w_1 = \dfrac{z+1}{z-1} $.
	\newpage
	Найдем, куда под действием отображения перейдут кривые:\\
	$ \Gamma_1: z = x,\ -1 \leqslant x \leqslant 1$ перейдет в луч. ($ 0 \mapsto -1 $)\\
	$ \Gamma_2: z = e^{i\phi},\ 0 \leqslant \phi \leqslant \pi$ перейдет в луч. ($ i \mapsto -i $)

	\begin{example}
		Найти отображение, которое переводит $ D_z $ в $ D_w $, где\\ $ D_z = \{ z\in\Cm: |z| < 1, |z-i| < 1 \}, \ D_w = \{ w\in\Cm: \Im w > 0 \}$

	\[ z_1 =  -\frac{\sqrt 3}{2} + \frac{i}{2},\ z_2 = \frac{\sqrt 3}{2} + \frac{i}{2} \]
	Отображение $ w_1 = \dfrac{z - z_1}{z-z_2} $ такое, что $ z_1 \mapsto 0, \ z_2 \mapsto \infty,$ тогда \\
	$ 0 \mapsto \dfrac{z_1}{z_2} = \dfrac{-\sqrt 3 + i}{\sqrt 3 + i} = -\dfrac{1}{2} + \dfrac{\sqrt 3i}{2} $\\
	$ i \mapsto \dfrac{i - z_1}{i - z_2} = \dfrac{-\sqrt 3 + i}{\sqrt 3 + i} = -\dfrac{1}{2} - \dfrac{\sqrt 3i}{2} $
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
