	В конце, отображением $ w = w^\frac{3}{2}_2 $ развернем угол.+7 917 835 16 19
	\begin{flalign*}
	&\text{Ответ: } w = -\left( \frac{2z+\sqrt 3 - i}{2z - \sqrt 3 - i}\right)^\frac{3}{2}&
	\end{flalign*}
	Общая схема:
	\begin{flalign*}
		&w_1 = \frac{z-z_1}{z-z_2}&\\
		&w_2 = e^{i\phi}w_1,\ \phi \in \R&\\
		&w = w_2^l,\ l \in \R&
	\end{flalign*}
	\begin{remark}
		$ z_1 $ и $ z_2 $ можно менять местами в выражении $ w_1 = \dfrac{z-z_2}{z-z_1} $
	\end{remark}
	\begin{example}
		Найти отображение, которое переводит $ D_z $ в $ D_w $, где\\ $ D_z = \Cm \setminus \{ z\in\Cm: \Im z = 0,\ x_1\leqslant\Re z \leqslant x_2 \}, \ D_w = \{ w\in\Cm: \Im w > 0 \}$
	\end{example}
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.5,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-0.5,-0.05) rectangle (0.75,0.05);
				\node[above left] at (-0.5,0) {$x_1$};
				\node[above right] at (0.75,0) {$x_2$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
			
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Отобразим точку $ x_1 $ в $ 0 $, а точку $ x_2 $ в $ \infty $. Получим $ w_1 = \dfrac{z - x_1}{z - x_2} $.\\ Третью точку: $ \dfrac{x_1+x_2}{2} \mapsto -1 $.
	\newpage 
	Получится левый вырез, его повернем на $ \pi $ отображением: $ w_2 = e^{i\phi}w_1,\ \phi = \pi. $
	В конце, развернем угол в два раза отображением: $ w = w_2^\frac{1}{2}$.
	\begin{flalign*}
		&\text{Ответ: } w = \left( \frac{z - x_1}{x_2 - z}\right)^\frac{1}{2}&
	\end{flalign*}
	\newpage
	
	\section{Лекция 13}
	\subsection{Отображение луночки на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	Строим отображение луночки на верхнюю полуплоскость:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\clip (-0.4,0) circle (1.2);
					\fill[blue!20] (0.4,0) circle (1.2);
				\end{scope}
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (-0.4,-1.2) arc (-90:90:1.2);
				\draw (0.4,-1.2) arc (270:90:1.2);
				\fill (0,{sqrt(1.2^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$z_1$};
				\fill (0,{-sqrt(1.2^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
		
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
		Для начала используем дробно-линейное отображение $w_1 = \dfrac{z - z_1}{z - z_2}$, где один из полюсов отправляем в 0, а другой в $\infty$
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\clip (-0.4,0) circle (1.2);
						\fill[blue!20] (0.4,0) circle (1.2);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (-0.4,-1.2) arc (-90:90:1.2);
					\draw (0.4,-1.2) arc (270:90:1.2);
					\fill (0,{sqrt(1.2^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$z_1$};
					\fill (0,{-sqrt(1.2^2-0.4^2)}) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$z_2$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}

				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (1.4096,0.513) arc (20:70:1.5) -- cycle;
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0,0) -- (1.4096,0.513);
					\draw (0,0) -- (0.513,1.4096);
						
					\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					\draw (0.5,0) arc (0:20:0.5);
					\node at (10:0.75) {$\alpha$};
					
					\draw (0.6578, 0.2394) arc (20:70:0.7);
					\node at (45:0.95) {$\beta$};
						
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
				\end{scope}
					
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
					
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_1$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
		Далее при помощи $w_2 = e^{-i\alpha} w_1$ поворачиваем на угол $\alpha$ по часовой.
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (1.4096,0.513) arc (20:70:1.5) -- cycle;
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0,0) -- (1.4096,0.513);
					\draw (0,0) -- (0.513,1.4096);
						
					\draw (0.5,0) arc (0:20:0.5);
					\node at (10:0.75) {$\alpha$};
					\draw (0.6578, 0.2394) arc (20:70:0.7);
					\node at (45:0.95) {$\beta$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (1.5,0) arc (0:50:1.5) -- cycle;
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0,0) -- (0.9642, 1.149);
					\draw (0.5,0) arc (0:50:0.5);
					\node at (0.7,0.25) {$\beta$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
				\end{scope}
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 1cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	На последнем шаге нужно раскрыть наш сектор из угла $\beta$ до угла $\pi$, используя отображение $w = w_2^{\frac{\pi}{\beta}}$:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) -- (1.5,0) arc (0:50:1.5) -- cycle;
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\draw (0,0) -- (0.9642, 1.149);						
					\draw (0.5,0) arc (0:50:0.5);
					\node at (0.7,0.25) {$\beta$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
				\end{scope}

				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
					
				\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\subsection{Отображение плоскости с выколотым отрезком на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	Строим отображение плоскости с выколотым отрезком $[z_1,\,z_2]$ на верхнюю полуплоскость:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						[rotate=-30] (-0.7,-0.05) rectangle (0.9,0.05);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (-0.6062,0.35) circle (0.5pt)node[above left] {$z_1$};
					\fill (0.7794,-0.45) circle (0.5pt)node[below right] {$z_2$};
					\fill (0.087, -0.05) circle (0.5pt)node[above right]{$\frac{z_1+z_2}{2}$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
				\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Используем дробно-линейное отображение $w_1 = \frac{z - z_1}{z - z_2}$. Отрезок $[z_1,\,z_2]$ переходит в луч. Проверим середину отрезка:
	\[\frac{z_1 + z_2}{2} \mapsto \frac{\frac{z_1+z_2}{2} - z_1}{\frac{z_1+z_2}{2} - z_2} = \frac{z_2 - z_1}{z_1 - z_2} = -1\]
	Значит, отрезок переходит в луч $(-\infty,\,0]$.
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						[rotate=-30] (-0.7,-0.05) rectangle (0.9,0.05);
					\end{scope}
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (-0.6062,0.35) circle (0.5pt)node[above left] {$z_1$};
					\fill (0.7794,-0.45) circle (0.5pt)node[below right] {$z_2$};
					\fill (0.087, -0.05) circle (0.5pt)node[above right]{$\frac{z_1+z_2}{2}$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						(-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (0,0.05);
					\end{scope}						
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$0$};
					\fill (-1,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$-1$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
				\end{scope}
					
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
				\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_1$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Разворачиваем луч при помощи $w_2 = e^{i\pi} w_1 = -w_1$. Луч $(-\infty, 0]$ переходит в $[0, +\infty)$:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						(-1.5,-0.05) rectangle (0,0.05);
					\end{scope}						
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$0$};
					\fill (-1,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$-1$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
				\end{scope}
					
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						(0,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
					\end{scope}	
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					\fill (1,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$1$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
				\end{scope}
					
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
				\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_2$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Наконец, извлекаем корень $w = w_2^{1/2}$. Луч $[0, +\infty)$ раскрывается в верхнюю полуплоскость:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					\begin{scope}
						\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
						(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
						(0,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
					\end{scope}	
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					\fill (1,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$1$};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
				\end{scope}
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
					
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
				\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\frac{z-z_1}{z_2-z}}$
	\newpage
	\subsection{Отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	Построить отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.05,0) rectangle (0.05,0.75);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (0,0.75) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
				\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
				
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] (startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Первым шагом возводим в квадрат: $w_1 = z^2$. Верхняя полуплоскость переходит в плоскость с разрезом вдоль горизонтальной оси. Вертикальный разрез $[0, ih]$ переходит в горизонтальный $[-h^2, +\infty)$:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.05,0) rectangle (0.05,0.75);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (0,0.75) circle (0.5pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
				\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below left] {$0$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.8,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (-0.8,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$-h^2$};	
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
			\end{scope}
					
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_1$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Сдвигаем разрез: $w_2 = w_1 + h^2$. Разрез $[-h^2, +\infty)$ переходит в $[0, +\infty)$:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(-0.8,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (-0.8,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$-h^2$};	
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_1$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(0,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below  left] {$0$};	
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w_2$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	Наконец, извлекаем корень $w = w_2^{1/2}$. Угол $2\pi$ сворачивается в верхнюю полуплоскость:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
				\begin{scope}
					\fill[blue!20, even odd rule] 
					(-1.5,-1.5) rectangle (1.5,1.5)
					(0,-0.05) rectangle (1.5,0.05);
				\end{scope}	
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\fill (0,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below  left] {$0$};	
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w_2$};
			\end{scope}
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
			
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1cm]scope2.west);
			\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0,1cm)$);
			\draw[->, thick] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$w$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
	\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{z^2 + h^2}$
	\subsection{Отображение полоски с вертикальным разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение верхней полуплоскости с вертикальным разрезом $[0, ih]$ и ограничением $i\alpha$ ($\alpha > h$) на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полосы
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Верхняя граница i\alpha
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до ih
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
					
					% Точка ih
					\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Растягиваем полосу: $w_1 = z \cdot \frac{\pi}{\alpha}$. Получаем полосу высоты $\pi$ с разрезом от $0$ до $ic$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Верхняя граница i\pi
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						% Разрез от 0 до ic
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ic$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{\pi}{\alpha} z$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Применяем экспоненту: $w_2 = e^{w_1}$. Полоса переходит в верхнюю полуплоскость с разрезом по дуге окружности от $1$ до $e^{ic}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.5,1.5) -- (1.5,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ic$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						% Верхняя полуплоскость с вырезанным сектором
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							% Вырезаем сектор (белая область)
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) -- (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3] -- cycle;
						\end{scope}
						
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Границы разреза (две дуги)
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0.05) arc[start angle=1, end angle=54, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,-0.05) arc[start angle=-1, end angle=52, radius=1.3];
						
						% Радиальные линии от 0 до дуги (границы сектора)
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819);
						
						% Единичная окружность (пунктиром)
						\draw[gray, dashed] (0,0) circle (1.3);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.3,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
						\fill[red] (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$e^{ic}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = e^{w_1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Дробно-линейное отображение $w_3 = \frac{w_2 - 1}{w_2 + 1}$ переводит разрез в вертикальный отрезок $[0, i\tan\frac{c}{2}]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) -- (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3] -- cycle;
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0) arc[start angle=0, end angle=55, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,0.05) arc[start angle=1, end angle=54, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (1.3,-0.05) arc[start angle=-1, end angle=52, radius=1.3];
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819);
						\draw[gray, dashed] (0,0) circle (1.3);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.3,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
						\fill[red] (1.3*0.574,1.3*0.819) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$e^{ic}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Вертикальный разрез (белая полоса с границами)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.65);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.65);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.65);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.65) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\tan\frac{c}{2}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = \frac{w_2-1}{w_2+1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Сводим к предыдущей задаче: $w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.6);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\tan\frac{c}{2}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$.
	\end{example}
	\newpage
	\subsection{Отображение полоски с вертикальным разрезом на полоску}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полосы высоты $\alpha$ с вертикальным разрезом $[0, ih]$ на полосу высоты $\alpha$ без разреза:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полосы
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Верхняя граница i\alpha
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до ih
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
					\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
					
					% Точка ih
					\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (полоса без разреза) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$w$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w_1 = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$. Это отображение переводит полосу с разрезом в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ih$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, font=\footnotesize] {$w_1 = \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Логарифмируем: $w_2 = \ln w_1$. Верхняя полуплоскость переходит в полосу высоты $\pi$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (полоса высоты \pi) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = \ln w_1$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Сжимаем полосу обратно: $w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} w_2$. Получаем полосу высоты $\alpha$ без разреза:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (полоса высоты \alpha) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$i\alpha$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,0.8) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} w_2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \frac{\alpha}{\pi} \ln \sqrt{\left(\frac{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} - 1}{e^{\frac{\pi z}{\alpha}} + 1}\right)^2 + \tan^2\frac{c}{2}}$, где $c = \frac{\pi h}{\alpha}$.
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение полуполосы с горизонтальным на разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полуполосы $\{z: \Re z > 0, 0 < \Im z < h\}$ с горизонтальным разрезом $[0, \alpha]$ на высоте $\frac{ih}{2}$ на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полуполоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полуполосы
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Левая граница (Re z = 0)
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					
					% Верхняя граница
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					% Горизонтальный разрез на высоте ih/2
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
					
					% Конец разреза
					\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Растягиваем: $w_1 = z \cdot \frac{\pi}{h}$. Получаем полуполосу высоты $\pi$ с разрезом от $0$ до $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$ на высоте $\frac{i\pi}{2}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
						\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						% Разрез на высоте i\pi/2
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.75) -- (1.0,0.75);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.73) -- (1.0,0.73);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.77) -- (1.0,0.77);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.0,0.75) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$c$};
						
						\node at (0,0.75) [left] {$\frac{i\pi}{2}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{\pi}{h} z$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Экспонента: $w_2 = e^{w_1}$. Полуполоса переходит во внешность единичной полуокружности с вертикальным разрезом от $i$ до $ie^c$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.5,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.75) -- (1.0,0.75);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.73) -- (1.0,0.73);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.77) -- (1.0,0.77);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (1.0,0.75) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.2) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (внешность полуокружности с вертикальным разрезом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							% Вырезаем нижний полукруг (единичная полуокружность)
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							% Вырезаем вертикальный разрез от i до i e^C
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						% Единичная полуокружность
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						
						% Вертикальный разрез от i до i e^C
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						
						% Точки -1 и 1 на вещественной оси
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = e^{w_1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Функция Жуковского: $w_3 = \frac{1}{2}\left(w_2 + \frac{1}{w_2}\right)$. Внешность полуокружности с разрезом переходит в верхнюю полуплоскость с вертикальным разрезом $[0, i\sh c]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 (верхняя полуплоскость с вертикальным разрезом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						% Вертикальный разрез от 0 до i sh C
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\sh c$};
						
						% Точки -1 и 1 на вещественной оси
						\fill[black] (-1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[black] (1.0,0) circle (0.8pt) node[below] {$1$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = \frac{1}{2}\left(w_2 + \frac{1}{w_2}\right)$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \sh^2 c}$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (0,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,0) -- (-0.05,0.7);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,0) -- (0.05,0.7);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,0.7) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i\sh c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.0) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \sqrt{w_3^2 + \sh^2 c}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c}$, где $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$.
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение полуполосы с горизонтальным разрезом на полуполосу без разреза}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение полуполосы $\{z: \Re z > 0,\ 0<\Im z<h\}$ с горизонтальным разрезом $[0, \alpha]$ на высоте $\frac{ih}{2}$ на полуполосу без разреза:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (полуполоса с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка полуполосы
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					% Левая граница (Re z = 0)
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					
					% Верхняя граница
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					% Горизонтальный разрез на высоте ih/2
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
					\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
					
					% Конец разреза
					\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
					
					% Обозначение 0
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (полуполоса без разреза) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
					\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
					\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
					\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center} 
		\newpage
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w_1 = \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c}$, где $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$. Это отображение переводит полуполосу с разрезом в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0.6) -- (0.8,0.6);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.58) -- (0.8,0.58);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.62) -- (0.8,0.62);
						\fill[red] (0.8,0.6) circle (1.2pt) node[above] {$\alpha$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, font=\footnotesize] {$w_1 = \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Обратная функция Жуковского: $w_2 = w_1 + \sqrt{w_1^2 - 1}$ (главная ветвь). Верхняя полуплоскость переходит во внешность единичной полуокружности с вертикальным разрезом от $i$ до $ie^c$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_2 = w_1 + \sqrt{w_1^2 - 1}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			\item Логарифмируем: $w_3 = \ln w_2$. Внешность полуокружности с разрезом переходит в полуполосу высоты $\pi$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,0) rectangle (1.8,1.8);
							\fill[white] (0,0) circle (1.0);
							\fill[white] (-0.05,1.0) rectangle (0.05,1.5);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.0);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (-0.05,1.0) -- (-0.05,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0.05,1.0) -- (0.05,1.5);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.0) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$i$};
						\fill[red] (0,1.5) circle (1.2pt) node[above right] {$ie^c$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.2,1.2) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 (полуполоса высоты \pi) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.8,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,1.2) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = \ln w_2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\newpage
			\item Сжимаем полуполосу: $w = \frac{h}{\pi} w_3$. Получаем полуполосу высоты $h$ без разреза:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.8) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.5);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.5) -- (1.5,1.5);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.5) {$i\pi$};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,1.2) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (полуполоса высоты h) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-0.3,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.3) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\draw[thick] (0,0) -- (0,1.2);
						\draw[thick] (0,1.2) -- (1.8,1.2);
						\node[above left] at (0,1.2) {$ih$};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.2,0.9) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \frac{h}{\pi} w_3$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \frac{h}{\pi} \ln\left( \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c} + \sqrt{\ch^2\left(\frac{\pi z}{h}\right) + \sh^2 c - 1} \right)$, где $c = \frac{\pi \alpha}{h}$.
	\end{example}
	\subsection{Отображение единичного круга с разрезом на верхнюю полуплоскость}
	\begin{example}
		Строим отображение единичного круга $\{z: |z| < 1\}$ с разрезом по отрезку $[h, 1]$ на верхнюю полуплоскость:
		\begin{center}
			\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
				% --- Область Z (круг с разрезом) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
					% Заливка круга
					\begin{scope}
						\clip (0,0) circle (1.2);
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,-1.2) rectangle (1.5,1.2);
					\end{scope}
					
					% Вырезаем разрез [h, 1]
					\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0.5,0) -- (1.2,0);
					\draw[thick] (0.5,0.03) -- (1.2,0.03);
					\draw[thick] (0.5,-0.03) -- (1.2,-0.03);
					
					% Оси
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
					
					% Окружность
					\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.2);
					
					% Точки
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					\fill[red] (0.5,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$h$};
					\fill[red] (1.2,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
					
					% Подпись области
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-0.8,0.7) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Область W (верхняя полуплоскость) ---
				\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
					\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
					\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
					
					\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
					
					\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
				\end{scope}
				
				% --- Стрелка ---
				\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
				\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
				\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
				
				\draw[->, thick] 
				(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
				node[midway, above] {$f$};
				
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{center}
		\begin{enumerate}
			\item Функция Жуковского: $w_1 = \frac{1}{2}\left(z + \frac{1}{z}\right)$. Отрезок $[h, 1]$ переходит в $[1, \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})]$, а окружность — в отрезок $[-1, 1]$. Получаем плоскость с разрезом $[-1, \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\begin{scope}
							\clip (0,0) circle (1.2);
							\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,-1.2) rectangle (1.5,1.2);
						\end{scope}
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0.5,0) -- (1.2,0);
						\draw[thick] (0.5,0.03) -- (1.2,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (0.5,-0.03) -- (1.2,-0.03);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.2);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (0.5,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$h$};
						\fill[red] (1.2,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-0.8,0.7) {$z$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W1 (плоскость с разрезом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						
						% Разрез [-1, 1.2] (где 1.2 соответствует \frac{1}{2}(h+1/h))
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.0,0) -- (1.2,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.0,0.03) -- (1.2,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (-1.0,-0.03) -- (1.2,-0.03);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (-1.0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[red] (1.2,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$\frac{1}{2}(h+\frac{1}{h})$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (0,0.8) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_1 = \frac{1}{2}\left(z + \frac{1}{z}\right)$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\newpage
			\item Дробно-линейное отображение: $w_2 = \frac{w_1 + 1}{w_1 - \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})}$. Точка $0$ переходит в $-\frac{2}{h + 1/h} < 0$, разрез $[-1, \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})]$ переходит в луч $(-\infty, 0]$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.0,0) -- (1.2,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.0,0.03) -- (1.2,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (-1.0,-0.03) -- (1.2,-0.03);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[red] (-1.0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-1$};
						\fill[red] (1.2,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$\frac{1}{2}(h+\frac{1}{h})$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (0,0.8) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W2 (плоскость с лучом) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						
						% Луч (-∞, 0]
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.8,0) -- (0,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,0.03) -- (0,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,-0.03) -- (0,-0.03);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (-0.6,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-\frac{2}{h+1/h}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,0.8) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, font=\footnotesize] {$w_2 = \frac{w_1 + 1}{w_1 - \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Разворачиваем луч: $w_3 = -w_2$. Луч $(-\infty, 0]$ переходит в $[0, +\infty)$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W2 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (-1.8,0) -- (0,0);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,0.03) -- (0,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (-1.8,-0.03) -- (0,-0.03);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (-0.6,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$-\frac{2}{h+1/h}$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (1.0,0.8) {$w_2$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						
						% Луч [0, +∞)
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.03) -- (1.8,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.03) -- (1.8,-0.03);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (0.6,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$\frac{2}{h+1/h}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,0.8) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w_3 = -w_2$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			\item Извлекаем корень: $w = \sqrt{w_3}$. Луч $[0, +\infty)$ раскрывается в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W3 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.8,-1.2) rectangle (1.8,1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.8,0) -- (1.8,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[white, line width=6pt] (0,0) -- (1.8,0);
						\draw[thick] (0,0.03) -- (1.8,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (0,-0.03) -- (1.8,-0.03);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\fill[blue] (0.6,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below] {$\frac{2}{h+1/h}$};
						
						% Обозначение берегов
						\node[above right] at (0.8,0.1) {$w_3 = r e^{i0}$};
						\node[below right] at (0.8,-0.1) {$w_3 = r e^{i2\pi}$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,0.8) {$w_3$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=4.5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.3cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \sqrt{w_3}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\end{enumerate}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \sqrt{-\frac{\frac{1}{2}(z + \frac{1}{z}) + 1}{\frac{1}{2}(z + \frac{1}{z}) - \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})}} = \sqrt{\frac{z^2 + 2z + 1}{-z^2 + (h + \frac{1}{h})z - 1}}$.
	\end{example}
	\newpage
	\subsection{Отображение единичного круга с разрезом на единичный круг}
	Строим отображение единичного круга $\{ z: |z| < 1 \}$ с разрезом по отрезку $[h, 1]$ на единичный круг без разреза:
	\begin{center}
		\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=2]
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]

					(0.3,-0.05) rectangle (1,0.05); 
				\end{scope}

				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
				\draw (0,0) circle (1);
				\fill (0.3,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below] {$h$};
				\fill (1,0) circle (0.5pt) node[below right] {$1$};
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$z$};
				\end{scope}
				
			\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
				\fill[blue!20] (0,0) circle (1);
				\draw (0,0) circle (1);
				\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
				\draw[->] (0,-1.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};			
				\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.3,1.3) {$w$};
			\end{scope}
				
			\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=1.2cm]scope1.east);
			\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1.0cm]scope2.west);

			\draw[->,thick, black!60!black, line width=1.2pt, shorten >=2pt, shorten <=-13pt] 
			(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
			node[midway, above, yshift=5pt] {$f$};
		\end{tikzpicture}
	\end{center}
			Используем результат предыдущей задачи: $w_1 = \sqrt{-\frac{\frac{1}{2}(z + \frac{1}{z}) + 1}{\frac{1}{2}(z + \frac{1}{z}) - \frac{1}{2}(h + \frac{1}{h})}} = \sqrt{\frac{z^2 + 2z + 1}{-z^2 + (h + \frac{1}{h})z - 1}}$. Это отображение переводит круг с разрезом в верхнюю полуплоскость:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область Z ---

							\clip (0,0) circle (1.2);

						\end{scope}

						\draw[thick] (0.5,0.03) -- (1.2,0.03);
						\draw[thick] (0.5,-0.03) -- (1.2,-0.03);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.2);
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};

						\fill[red] (1.2,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below right] {$1$};

						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=0.3cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above, font=\footnotesize] {$w_1 = \sqrt{\frac{z^2 + 2z + 1}{-z^2 + (h + \frac{1}{h})z - 1}}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
			
			Отображаем верхнюю полуплоскость в единичный круг: $w_2 = \frac{w_1 - i}{w_1 + i} \cdot K$, где $K = e^{i\alpha}$, $\alpha = 0$:
			\begin{center}
				\begin{tikzpicture}[scale=1.8]
					% --- Область W1 ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope1]
						\fill[blue!20] (-1.5,0) rectangle (1.5,1.5);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,1.5) node[above] {};
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-1.0,1.0) {$w_1$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Область W (круг) ---
					\begin{scope}[local bounding box=scope2, xshift=5cm]
						\fill[blue!20] (0,0) circle (1.2);
						\draw[->] (-1.5,0) -- (1.5,0) node[right] {};
						\draw[->] (0,-1.2) -- (0,1.2) node[above] {};
						\draw[thick] (0,0) circle (1.2);
						
						\fill[red] (0,0) circle (1.2pt) node[below left] {$0$};
						
						\node[draw, circle, inner sep=2pt, fill=white] at (-0.8,0.7) {$w$};
					\end{scope}
					
					% --- Стрелка ---
					\coordinate (startArrow) at ([yshift=0.8cm]scope1.east);
					\coordinate (endArrow) at ([yshift=1.4cm]scope2.west);
					\coordinate (midArrow) at ($(startArrow)!0.5!(endArrow) + (0, 0.6cm)$);
					
					\draw[->, thick] 
					(startArrow) .. controls ($(startArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) and ($(endArrow)!0.4!(midArrow)$) .. (endArrow)
					node[midway, above] {$w = \frac{w_1 - i}{w_1 + i}$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{center}
		\textbf{Ответ:} $w = \frac{\sqrt{\frac{z^2 + 2z + 1}{-z^2 + (h + \frac{1}{h})z - 1}} - i}{\sqrt{\frac{z^2 + 2z + 1}{-z^2 + (h + \frac{1}{h})z - 1}} + i}$.
	\section{Лекция 14}
	\subsection{Интегрирование функций комплексного переменного.}
	Дана гладкая или кусочно-гладкая кривая $ \gamma $ и её разбиение $\tau = \{A = z_0,\, z_1, \ldots,\, z_n = B \}$. На каждом $\Delta z_k = z_k - z_{k-1}$ берем опорную точку $\xi_k \in \gamma.\ \xi = \{ \xi_1,\, \ldots,\, \xi_n \} $.
	Параметр разбиения $ \lambda = \max\limits_{1 \leqslant k 
	\leqslant n}|\Delta z_k|$. Пусть $f(z)$ --- однозначная функция, определенная на прямой $\gamma$. Составим интегральную сумму: $\sigma(f,\, \xi,\, \tau) = \Sum_{k=1}^n f(\xi_k)\Delta z_k$.
	\begin{definition}
		Пусть при $ \lambda \rightarrow 0 $ существует конечный предел интегральной суммы и этот предел не зависит от выбора разбиения и точек $ \xi $, тогда его обозначают $ \int_\gamma f(z)dz $ и называют \textbf{интегралом} от функции $ f(z) $ по кривой $ \gamma $ в выбранном направлении.
		\[ \Int_\gamma f(z)\,dz = \Lim_{\lambda\rightarrow 0}\ \Sum_{k=1}^n f(\xi_k)\Delta z_k. \]
	\end{definition}
	Дано параметрическое представление прямой $ \gamma: (x(t),\,y(t)),\ t \in [a,\,b] $.\\ Тогда по Т. Пифагора(физический уровень строгости): $ ds = \sqrt{dx^2+dy^2} = \sqrt{x'^2+y'^2}\,dt$.\\
	\textbf{Криволинейный интеграл 1-го рода:}
	\[ I_1 =  \Int_\gamma f(z)\,ds = \Int_\alpha^\beta f(x(t),\,y(t))\sqrt{x'^2+y'^2}\,dt \]
	\textbf{Криволинейный интеграл 2-го рода:}
	\[ I_2 =  \Int_\gamma \bar g(x,\,y)\,d\bar s = \Int_\gamma Pdx + Qdy = 
	\Int_\alpha^\beta (P(x,\,y)x' + Q(x,\,y)y')\,dt, \]
	где $ d\bar s = (dx,\, dy),\quad \bar g(x,\,y) = (P(x,\,y),\ Q(x,\,y)) $
	\begin{theorem}
		Пусть существуют криволинейные интегралы 2-го рода: $\Int_\gamma vdx + udy,\ \Int_\gamma udx - vdy $. Тогда\\
		\[ \Int_\gamma f(z)\,dz = \Int_\gamma udx - vdy + i\Int_\gamma vdx + udy \]
	\end{theorem}
	\begin{proof}
		\[ \Int_\gamma f(z)\,dz = \Lim_{\lambda\rightarrow 0}\ \Sum_{k=1}^n f(\xi_k)\Delta z_k = \Lim_{\lambda\rightarrow 0}\ \Sum_{k=1}^n (u(\xi_k) + iv(\xi_k))(\Delta x_k + i\Delta y_k) = \]
		\[ = \Lim_{\lambda\rightarrow 0}\ \Sum_{k=1}^n(u(\xi_k)\Delta x_k - v(\xi_k)\Delta y_k) + i\Lim_{\lambda\rightarrow 0}\ \Sum_{k=1}^n(v(\xi_k)\Delta x_k + u(\xi_k)\Delta y_k) \]
	\end{proof}
	\begin{theorem}
		Пусть $f(z) \in C(\gamma)$, где $\gamma$ --- гладкая кривая Жордана,  $ z = z(t),\ t \in [\alpha,\,\beta] $. Тогда
		\[ \Int_\gamma f(z)\,dz = \Int_\alpha^\beta f(z(t))z'(t)\,dt. \]
	\end{theorem}
	\begin{proof}
		$ f(z) \in C(\gamma) \Rightarrow u(x, y),\ v(x, y) \in C(\gamma) $. По определению кривой Жордана: $ x(t),\ y(t) \in C^1[\alpha,\,\beta],\ z(t)= x(t) + iy(t),\ dz = (x' + iy')dt $
		\begin{align*}
		J_1 = \Int_\gamma udx-vdy = \Int_\alpha^\beta u(x(t),\, y(t))x'(t)- v(x(t),\, y(t))y'(t)\,dt\\
		J_2 = \Int_\gamma udx+vdy = \Int_\alpha^\beta u(x(t),\, y(t))x'(t)+ v(x(t),\, y(t))y'(t)\,dt\\
		\Int_\gamma f(z)\,dz = J_1 + iJ_2 = \Int_\gamma(u+iv)(x'(t) + iy'(t))\,dt = \Int_\alpha^\beta f(z(t))z'(t)\,dt
		\end{align*}
	\end{proof}
	\begin{example}			
			\begin{minipage}{0.4\textwidth}
				\[ 1)\ I = \Int_\gamma z\Re z\,dz \]
			\end{minipage}
			\begin{minipage}{0.4\textwidth}
				\begin{tikzpicture}
					\draw[->] (-0.5,0) -- (3,0) node[below] {$x$};
					\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,3) node[left] {$y$};
					\draw(0,0) -- (2.5,1.7);
					\draw[dashed] (2.5,1.7) -- (2.5,0);
					\draw[dashed] (2.5,1.7) -- (0,1.7);
					\fill (2.5,1.7) circle (1pt);
					\node[below] at (2.5,0) {$2$};
					\node[left] at (0,1.7) {$1$};
					\node[left] at (1.2,1) {$\gamma$};
				\end{tikzpicture}
			\end{minipage}
	\end{example}
	Выполним параметризацию кривой $ \gamma : z = x + i\dfrac{x}{2},\ x \in [0,\,2].\ dz = 1+\dfrac{i}{2}\,dx $
	\[ I =  \Int_0^2 \left( x+i\frac{x}{2}\right)x\left( 1+ \frac{i}{2} \right) dx = \left( 1+ \frac{i}{2} \right)^2\Int_0^2 x^2\,dx = \left.\left( \frac{3}{4} + i \right) \frac{x^3}{3}\,\right|_0^2 = 2 + \frac{8}{3}i. \]
	\begin{example}			
		\begin{minipage}{0.4\textwidth}
			\[ 2)\ I = \Int_\gamma\Im z\,dz \]
		\end{minipage}
		\begin{minipage}{0.4\textwidth}
			\begin{tikzpicture}
				\draw[->] (-3,0) -- (3,0) node[below] {$x$};
				\draw[->] (0,-0.5) -- (0,3) node[left] {$y$};
				\draw (-2,0) arc (180:0:2) -- cycle;
				\node[left] at (1.6, 2) {$\gamma$};
				\node[below] at (2, 0) {$1$};
			\end{tikzpicture}
		\end{minipage}
	\end{example}
	Выполним параметризацию кривой $\gamma: z = e^{it},\ t \in [0,\,\pi].\ dz = ie^{it}\,dt$
